dou poil qui point l’oil	the hairs that do not oil
Aucune fois avient que li poil des oilz sont convertit au pardedens, et poignent l’oil, et i fait on cauteres selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir de feu, ou de medicine ardant.	Never has it happened that the hairs of the oiled ones are converted to the parchedens, and they oil, and then one applies cauteries in two ways: that is to say, by fire, or by burning medicine.
Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals; et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il naissent et i sont igalz, adonques met le malaide en ton sain; aprés seigne sus la papiere des eulz une figure que soit ausi com li fuelle dou mirte, et soit li comencemens dou signe delez les poilz; puis i met coton moilliet en glaire d’uef et muscillaige de persillion sus l’oil, puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When they grow long and even, then prick the hairs; afterwards place a piece of paper under the eyes to hold them steady; then put soft cotton moistened with eagle's oil and musk on the wound, then heat the fire cauterization in the form:
Aprés cauterize sus la figure que tu as signiet poc et poc mout de fois, que li keurs soit ars lai endroit; et li signes de la santeit de l’uevre est que tu voies la papiere retraite, et les poilz levez a la pointure de l’oil; adonques lieve ta main, et laisse ensi III jors, puis i met coton moilliet en burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cauterize slowly and gently a few times, until the pain is less intense in that place; and the sign of the work's health is that you see the paper retreat, and the hairs stand upright; then remove your hand, and leave it thus for three hours, then put soft cotton moistened with butter until the burn is healed; afterwards treat the wound with ointment until it is healthy.
Et se aprés ceu vienent li poilz, et li papiere est mollifie adonques rencomence le cautere sus cel leu meisme, si com tu as fait premiers; et se li poil sont defuer, si le cauterize tant que li papiere soit levee a son leu natureil, et soit igals, et ne poignent mie li poil l’oil.	And if after this the hairs come back, and the paper is softened, then begin the cauterization again on the same spot, as you did before; and if the hairs are lacking, then cauterize until the paper is raised to its natural level, and is even, and do not prick at the hair with it.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient grans et igalz, puis fai de parchemin la forme de la foille de mirte; puis pren de savon fransois et de vive chalz, de chescun une .З., et broie ensamble bien; et le fai hastanment, si qu’il ne refroide, puis en espant sus la forme que tu es fait sicom la foille dou mirte, et met sus la papiere des eulz; et se li maladie tient en I oil soulement, si doit on ovrer en I, et se en ambedous ausi; et met desoz l’oil coton moilliet en abin d’uef; et li chiés dou malaide soit en ton sain et met ton doi mostrant sus la medicine, et presse I poc et lou muef toutes les fois que li malaide sent mordication de la medicine, car il sent mordication ausi com de feu.	The cauterization of medicine with fire is that you command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; then take a piece of parchment in the shape of a myrtle leaf; then take French soap and live quartz, one of each, and grind them together well; and apply it strongly, so that it does not cool, then spread it on the form you have made like the myrtle leaf, and place it on the paper at the eyes; and if the patient's illness is only in one eye, then cover only that one, and do the same for the other; and place a piece of soft cotton cloth underneath to prevent burning; and the patient should be in a healthy state and show the medicine, and press the poultice every time the patient feels the burning sensation of the medicine, because it feels like fire.
Quant tu as ceu fait longement, si oste la medicine a ton doit.	When you have done this for a long time, then take the medicine to your mouth.
Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision; et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	And when the blister has burst, lift the limb upwards, and rewarm it if you see the paper rising as it was raised by constraint of fire or by incision; and if so, it is well.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point; puis met sus coton moilliet en burre tant que li keurs ars soit cheus, aprés cure le leu de l’oignement qui est apelez «dyafenis» et d’autre, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If not, still apply the medicine above the limb or where the medicine has not worked, until your work is even, and your eyes are set; then put moist cotton on the wound until the curses are chosen, after care, the limb of the ointment which is called «dyafenis» and others, until it is healed.
Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	And if you have the duty to stay well within your work, by great care that it does not pierce through the medicine with those.
Et se li papiere devient mole aprés, et li poil poignent en l’oil, si recomence la medicine sus celui leu qui est mollifiez de la papiere proprement, ensi com tu as fait devant; aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	And if the paper becomes soft afterwards, and the hairs prick in the oil, then restart the medicine on that one which is softened by the proper paper, as you have done before; then cure until it is healed; and this is the form of the fuel of the mire:
Et saichés que li eul des homes sont divers en grandor et en petitece, et selonc ceu soit tes constraignemens; et ne soit mie reponue li droite voie a celui cui est li estude de cest art.	And since the sizes of men's hairs are different in greatness and smallness, and according to what your constraints are; and do not return the right way to that one who is the study of this art.
de la cure de fistule par cautere	of the treatment of a fistula with cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat a fistula as we have mentioned in the division of diseases, and your treatments do not work, then it is necessary to cauterize it in this way.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain; et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief; aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil; aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz: et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere; se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente; mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	Command the patient to place his head in your safe hands; and bind his head between your hands in such a way that it does not move, nor move his head; afterward, put cotton moilliet behind the ear or on the side of persillion above the oil; after heating the cauterizer which is there: and fasten it to the head as if it were the form of a pen of vouteul, just like that which is the cauterizer; if you see, so it is appointed from one head to the other, and if you see, so it is also like a tent; but whatever, this which is fastened is good for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche; et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe; aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie; et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	After pressing the fistula, it is opened, and the pus is removed and dried; if it is closed, open it again, and scrape out the inside of the bowels; after that, apply the cauterizer hot and evenly, and hold your hand on the cauterizer at the part of the neck below the oil, so that your hand does not cause harm; and put the cauterizer into the oil grease, and corrupt it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cauterizer at the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors; aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers; et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	If not, if you have experience, and let it lie for three days; after that, put on a piece of soft cotton in butter, and the ointment of desiccating until it is healed, and if forty days pass without being healed, then put on corrosive medicine until the bone is discovered; and the king according to what he would come in his chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a method of cauterizing a fistula that no one of the ancients said.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu; aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	To the fistula, and close the wound; after put in the fissure some subtle powder of which this is the form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc; et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil; et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe: li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	And they make of the quantity of one drachm of pitch; and hold your hand or the powder firmly, and do not move the hairs until the pitch melts and does not spread to the oil; and it is necessary to put above the oil on the hair cotton moistened with water or oil: the pitch heals the wound of the fistula, and the skin by marvelous health.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the sinus is healed by the fire cautery that we have mentioned, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then one must administer poultices to the throat, and bring the sinus back to its proper place in the throat according to what is fitting for it.
des crevaices en levres	of cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Many times there are cracks in the lips that are called "hair", and at the same time in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have mentioned in the chapter on divisions, and the treatment does not help, then heat a small cauterizing needle according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font; aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And put the patient in those cracks until he comes just to the point of fainting; after that, care for the broken limb with plaster until it is healed.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the throat
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule; et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie: adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule; aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu; et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez; et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	When an abscess comes at the root of the throat or in the eye, or in the palate, or in the roots of the teeth, after it has putrefied and rotted and become aged and turned into a fistula; and if you cure it as we have said in divisions, it does not improve: then it is necessary that you use the cauterization according to the quantity of the fistula; afterwards, plug or puncture the fistula, and keep your hand there until the hot iron reaches the end of the limb, and behind the limb; and do thus once or twice, after caring for it as we have said in cures, until it is healed; and if it is cured thus, it is good; and if not, if necessary, you must expose the limb and remove the rotten bone, according to what you find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	movement of the teeth
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain; aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent; et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent; aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit; aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you treat them with medicines but it does not work, then put the tip of a sharp, heated iron in your mouth; place the hot iron on the tooth; hold your hand steady so that the pain feels the heat coming to the root of the tooth; then remove your hand and restart the iron according to your will; then fill the patient's mouth with salt water, and let them rinse for an hour and spit it out.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in a similar manner, the tooth that was moving is confirmed, and the gum softened by restraint, and the moisture corrupted dried.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres: et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	When pain from the teeth comes from coldness, or there is cold or wind, and medical remedies do not help, then it is necessary to use cauterization in two ways: cauterization with butter and cauterization with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain; aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez; et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	Cauterization with butter is such that you take butter from a freshly killed animal, and the end in an iron or brass spoon; afterward take cotton and wrap it around the point of a tent, and moisten it in hot butter, and place it on the painful tooth firmly and hold it until it is cooled; and thus do often enough until its power reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that moistened wool and cotton in hot butter is placed on the aching tooth, and place the heated iron over it until the fire comes to the movement of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide; aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez; fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	If the cautery is such that you hold a hot iron or copper, and it is large enough that the heat does not reach the mouth of the wound; after heating the cautery, because of which the wound will form afterwards, and put it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cautery is cooled; do this often, for the pain will be as great that same day or the next.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And it is necessary that the wound fill its mouth with good butter in the urgency of this cautery, and then the rinse; and this is the form of the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir; et c’est li forme de la caine:	And apply the fire cautery to the head that you wish, and according to what you have at hand; and this is the form of the knife:
des scrophules	of scalpels
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie; et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume; et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors; et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee; aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the scalpels are thin and cold, and do not obey digestion by medicines, then heat the fire cautery of head with this form, and have two openings for the fumes to issue from the other side; and put the fire cautery hot on the abscess once, or as often as it approaches the bottom of the abscess; and if the abscess is small, put the fire cautery according to the quantity of the abscess, and leave it thus for three days; and put wool moistened in butter over the burn until the sore is opened; afterward care for the wound with ointments and tents until it is healed.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the skull:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives; aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	When moisture overcomes the channels of the body, and especially when it comes from a cold complexion, then it is necessary to first remove the hairs by medicines that dissolve; after that, apply cauterization at the root of the throat, and do not come too close to the throat, and do not burn too much but with a small amount.
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant; et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	After that, apply another cauterization at the joint of the neck to the top of the spine, and let the cauterizer that is called "clavile" because of which we have the form in front; and cure the limb as we have said before until it is healed.
de la toust	of the mouth
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai ij cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis; et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles; et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	When all and the disease of the mouth are from cold moisture, and the pains have no fever or sweat, and this is an ancient disease, then make two cautery burns on the forceps in their own eyes; and the other cauteries emmi the worst between the two breasts; and let the cauteries that are called «clavile» according to the form that is before said.
Et se tu vues, fai cautere en poignant a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins» de coi li forme est ci devant en la maladie des oreilles; et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	And if you see, make cauteries by holding the entire cautery that is called «poins» because of the form that is above in the disease of the ears; and let the poins be just a little less than 30, or around.
Aprés cure le leu selonc ceu qui est devant dit, et soit li cauteres a III rains selonc ceste forme:	After treatment, the patient according to what has been said before, and let the burns be cauterized with three applications of this form:
Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais III a cop.	And because the cauteries are lighter, because you make three at a time.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the shoulder dislocation
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit; aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre; et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	After, shave the hairs on the back and on the side; then relieve the pain in the area of the tenderness with your right hand; and if the joint is misaligned inside, heat the cauteries that have two needles in this form:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres; et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres; et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	and cauterize the wound until it pierces just to the costal, and bring the four cauteries together; and because of this, the cauterization is made with the cauterizer that has three needles, because the figure of cauterization is these four needles; and they are the nerves according to the subtlety of a tent and it is the form of the cauterizer that has three needles.
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And sometimes they are placed on this one nerve because there are eight cauterizers.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil; aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After put the cauterizer on the broken parts; after rest the wound, and do not move the limbs by long tension until it is well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated above, this thing happens quickly, then make a cautery above the thick edge of the cautery, or many cauteries in pinching.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and it is stiff with moisture and is free from pain.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When cold and much moisture come to the stomach until it reaches its condition, and they multiply the diarrhea in him, and are customary methods of cures and he does not improve, then it is necessary that the pains be soothed above his back, and extends his legs and hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture; et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	After that, apply three cauteries on the tongue with a thin probe, as much as the quantity of one drop, to all the cautery clavile, and two cauteries afterwards on the two ribs until the figure of the cauteries is at three angles, and have equal space between them so that they are not joined together when they move; and let the cautery be so sharp that it pierces both sides of the tongue, and let the figure of the cauteries be in this form without twisting:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme; et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche; puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if you see that the cauterization is done with a great cautery in the stomach according to this form; and the one who has fear of this cautery, cauterizes by holding and looking up at the stomach i. point according to the quantity that you see of it; then cauterize all the cautery which is called «poins».
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the care of the care that we have had before, as long as they are healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez; et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil; et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient; et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi; et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere; et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez; et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais; et c’est li forme:	When the liver comes with pain from heat and moisture and great swelling, as long as it is not removed from its natural complexion by excess; and the hairs are treated as we have said in divisions, and it does not help them much, so it is necessary that the hairs be above their hairline; and the sign of three cauteries according to this form and figure and quantity above the liver, below the hypochondres, where the ears of the ox come; and there should be a space between each cauterization the thickness of one; and the cauterizations should be long as the length of the body, and do not press much with your hand throughout the cauterization; and it should be applied only to the half of the belly, and the hairs should be straight up; and if he cannot, then let him lie down, and extend his legs, and raise his arms; and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors; et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	And if you wish to cauterize these cauteries with a cutting instrument, if you are skilled and wise in the art, and you watch that you do not burn all the surrounding area, for you would make it harder all over; and that it does not come close to boiling, for the wounds are very delicate in that place, and the skilled ones must see.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile: s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort; et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	When he has an abscess in the liver, and you see whether it is in the flesh of the liver or in the membrane: if it is in the flesh, he does not feel much pain; and if it is in the membrane, he feels sharp pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste; et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	When this treatment is over, it is necessary that the wound be covered with a bandage; then apply a poultice to the affected area, and then heat the cauterizing iron which is similar to a thorn, because of this:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers; aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez; et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	Then cauterize the wound until the pus is all out; after the treatment according to the treatment of swellings as long as they are healthy; and it is only necessary to use this cauterizing iron for those who have studied long in the art of medicine, and by whose hands these diseases have never been corrupted.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Therefore, it can be boldly done, and it seems to me that it is worth leaving it alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	the fire cauterization
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere: pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois; et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe; et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc; et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules; et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	The ancients said that one should use the cauterization of aristolochia roots, and in this way: take a long aristolochia root, the longest you can find, and dry it, and as thick and long as your finger; and moisten it in oil, and take the cautery to the fire, and cauterize the cautery between the eyebrow and the forehead, and two small cauteries a little down on the part that is outside the beard; and two cauteries between the shoulder blade and the spine, leaning back a little; and one cautery underneath, and one above the stomach, and one between the shoulders, and two on the lower part in front of the cautery that is between the shoulders; and do not press your hand, but open it as if smelling.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme; et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	And no one said any ancient man that no man used a fire cauterizer similar to a razor, and they would scrape it and put it between the ribs, until it came to an abscess; and the pain was so great, as we have said in the liver abscess.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work, there is fear or the pain kills now, or a fistula comes that cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the mouse disease that we have said in the divisions of treatments, and it does not improve, then they try three methods of cauterization that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	When there is a certain way that you make three or four cauteries, lining up according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the cauterizing iron that we have mentioned before; and do not press your hand all over the cauterizing iron, and let the hairs be on its back; and another way of cauterizing is that you heat the cauterizing iron with two needles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder; and relieve the part where the hairs are located, or where the pain comes from the left side, and let the elevations that you relieve the part according to its curve, according to the length of the body, and the cauterizing iron should be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	After boiling the two needles until the curve is perceived from the other side, then remove the caustic, and thus enter into it with four. And if you see, then cauterize the whole caustic with three needles.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has gotten putrefaction by long time, and this is useful that the other of the treatments before said.
de ydropisie	of hydropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Caustic does not help with hydropsy, except in the manner which is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat it according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the belly, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the spleen, and one behind the back above the spine, and one at the worst place; and let the cauteries be close to the part that is most affected.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After leaving the cauterizer open for too long, and not letting the care of the wound after the cauterization rest, and healing would rush, and together with God's help, the two intentions would be accomplished.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The form of the cauterizer for the belly is like the one we have shown before; and for the back, it is an oil lamp, as it is written before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the feet are swollen to the one who is hydroptic, and they are plain of a yellowish wound, you must cauterize above the foot between the auricular and the anular; and let your hand with the cauterizer towards returning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, thus avoiding the sharp edges, and let the cauteries be done according to this form:

de la menoison	of the bandage

de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the flesh which is called "thelul

When you cut into the "thelul", if the heated cautery seems like a razor, and then put it all on fire over the cut "thelul"; and let your hand as far as the cauterizer comes to the birth of the vein, from which there is no bleeding; do this once or twice, and if there is much "thelul", cauterize each one as we have said; after curing the wounds until they are healthy; and if you cauterize with a large cautery high on the "thelul", it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of a poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wounds cannot be treated by a surgeon or opened, we will tell you what to do in such cases, as there is an illness that cannot be cured except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any fistula comes, and it is alert and poured with pus and corrupted moisture, then you should apply a thin tenture to it all, and make sure to remove the tenture as much as possible when it becomes full.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After heating the cautery that seems like a razor, and pushing it into the fistula according to the amount that the tenture has entered, and restarting the cauterization as long as the wound is still bleeding and corrupted, once or twice, or three times, depending on the amount of blood loss; and be careful not to burn the nerves that are nearby, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and the intestine, if you do not take care of these parts, and only treat where it is needed, and think that it is not healed; after treating the part as long as it is healthy, and if the parts are sewn together, and the matters are removed along with the tension, then the part is healed completely; and if the matters are not removed, then sew the part together, and corrode the bone at the fontanelle; and thus like one of those that we will say in its part.
de la maladie des reins	of the kidney disease

de la vessie	of the bladder

de la marris	of the marsh

de la hainche	Of the waist
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When viscous moisture descends to the waist bone, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the muscles of the buttocks are torn, then you should cauterize the injury above the waist bone with a cautery resembling a circle, and sign it around the bone as it turns, so that the bone is inside the circle; and if it is such a cauterization as has been used for the stomach.

de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the waist

When pain comes to the waist, and it is from cold and moisture, and the evils are caused by what we have said in the division and the cure does not help, and the disease is ancient: then it is necessary that you purge the evil of the large humors with fetid pills, or other good-smelling pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization; and the manner of the cauterization is as follows: it is to say together with burning medicines, and fire cauterization.

Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, the cautery is applied with a circular cauterizer as we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the shoulder; but do it in such a way that the circle contains the entire shoulder, and all the tendons should be included.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in lumbar puncture, when the pain remains in the shoulder and does not reach the thigh or leg.

And if it comes to the thigh and leg, then apply two cauterizers where the hairs indicate that the pain is located, and one cautery at the ankle four fingers wide, on the right side; and let the cauterizing knife cut through the tendon; and let the thickness of the tendon be included. And if the patient feels that the pain extends to two or three inches or near the knee, then cauterize where the pain is felt three or four times at the cautery called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the profession is, then do more; and if the pain is dislocated from the groin towards the thigh, then cauterize with a cauterizing or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not leave the cautery too long, burning the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I have also seen many who cauterized above the ankle of the foot, and left it too long that the leg was completely gangrenous, and the foot also, and all the feet were rotten and corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a bout of vomiting, which resulted in death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is on both sides together, perform cauterization on both, as follows.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And in the cauterization of the loins, this is how it should be done: use such a knife and make it as thick as a navillon of a thumb, or slightly less, and make it into a hook and insert it between the ribs and make it crosswise from one side to the other, with the length of a new penny; and the hooks should be above two parts, and they should also be like needles, and there should be a good handle.

And let it be heated until it is completely red and has a metallic scent, and then place it on the back of the misaligned shoulder, and turn it over to the healthy side; and cauterize once with the cautery and leave it for three days; and then apply a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time; after the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasis says that we use this cautery little because of its fearsome appearance, and few see those who use it; however, it is a good cautery that can bear much, and where it takes effect.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The cauterizing instrument of fiery medicine is such that you make a tool with notches on the edge of the door frame, and it is either of brass or iron at one end, and at the top, it has two prongs, and each has an amount of grease of a dog; and they are open below and above, and they join together according to this form:

ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant. Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés. And he said in a similar manner that you should take a small amount of fresh and dry turnip and grind it thoroughly with a little grease, and put it on the back and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is, and wrap it; and leave it for three hours until the hairs no longer feel the burn.

Then let the patient enter a warm bath until the body is slightly warmed up, and then let them lie down, and the pain will disappear completely and they will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And it should be noted that no one should use such cauterizing medicines unless after the evacuation of blood.

And Dioscorides says that when the vein is sciatic and is cauterized with the horn of a goat, it helps greatly; and it should be done in this way by the cauterizers.

Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After taking dry goat fleece, and placing it on fire until it becomes charcoal, and putting it on the wound, and leaving it there until it is soaked; and then repeating this process, and not ceasing to do so until you think by sense that it comes near to the skin, and that the pain has ceased; and this method of cauterization is called "goat's fleece cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	of double pain.
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or by impact or from too great evacuation, or from similar expanded cold matter, none of these remedies is effective, because it is for those who have recently undergone an infusion of cold matter.

After healing the limb as long as it is healthy according to what we have said, and ensure that you do not administer fire cautery in a place where there is a spasm of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in the joints is caused by moisture that has spread to each limb of the body, and when pain comes suddenly, which is properly called "gout", and when it is caused by cold and medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in this way: apply a large amount of cauterizing agent around the joint, and let the cauterizing oil be applied according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a gap where you can grip the joint, then apply cauterization to the entire cauterizing agent called "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pain comes from the knees and other joints, and it often occurs, then apply cauterization to each knee with three or four cauterizing agents of each part, to the entire cauterizing oil; and if you have more skill, then do more, but do not hold your hand further than the end of the curved part of the bone.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the groin and back, then administer the cautery that we have mentioned in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, make small incisions two lines wide; and if there is no pain at the wrist, make small incisions on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come from the elbow or shoulder, cauterize each part, and give good governance to the patient and many medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good governance and purge the humor, it will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the breaking of a tooth
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the breaking occurs in anger, and the saliva descends to the mouth and this is unusual, so it is necessary that when you see the tooth broken, do not move it on that day; and use things that draw out the bile, such that the feeling of nausea decreases from his stomach; afterwards make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to hold his jaw until the saliva has returned, and pull them with your fingers, and sign over the break above the bone of the little finger, and at all a sign that is similar to half a circle above the chest; then apply the cautery in this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	as long as it is white and sheds senselessness.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the mud from its joints; and the ministers stain their hands above so they do not return back; and work well on the thighs at the misalignment, and put disinfectant on him the cussin and the serjant above the thighs, and the other above the lowest that stains his hands; then put the cauterization above the sign of all your hand, and the right and the left as far as you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, start again another until you come close to the bone; and be careful that the mud does not come out when you do the cauterization; that you do not burn it; and that by this the pain does not kill him, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And when you do not cut to the bone with the fire cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And the cauterizer for children should be thin according to their age, and for adults as thick according to their size; after three days care for the wound with butter until the burn is healed; then care for other ailments until it is healthy, and let the hairs grow long on its back until the wound is well-healed; and it should be shaved a long time before going into rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty days, when he wishes to rise, apply a well-made bandage to him for forty more days; and let him have good rest, working little and avoiding too much drinking and eating, and too much noise; and if he follows this instruction, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will tell you after the cure of cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, then apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let the third part of the wound heal; after the cure according to what we have said; and none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with the fire cautery at three angles in this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but the first sign is the shoulder hunch and make a line across the width of the fracture, and another below, and hold your hand to all the cauterizing clamp.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and less painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any limb, whether to fall or to be injured, and this pain lasts long, and the medical cure does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize with the cauterizing iron called «poins», and the cauteries should be according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its strength and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If it is not healed with the first cautery, then start another cautery on top of the previous one, as it is customary that it should die to the member that is closest, because it is necessary to make the cauteries until the pain is healed.
de meselerie	I'm sorry, I don't have enough context to provide
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	These are never healed by cauterization with great help, and at the same time the disease that comes from the putrefaction of pus and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	If you see that the cauterization is not healing, take precautions if the disease is at the beginning, and if it has been cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not disappear or stay, and you doubt that the corruption will not spread throughout the pain, then make four cauterizations: I on the forehead, and the other towards the front at the end of the eyebrows; II above the two eyes, and I behind the ears; and leave as much hand as the cauterization comes to the bone, and as much as the scabs come out so that the vapors of the large humors can escape; and cauterize the mouth according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And if the infection is spread throughout; and it is obviously present, so you must cauterize with these cautery we have mentioned or chief, and the cauterization is in the lower nose, and two above the spine of the neck, and six above the spine of the back, and one great one and one other below, and two above the shoulders, and two above the elbows, and two above the knees, and one above each joint of the hands and feet, and above the wounds of the hands; and be careful of those that are above the back calcifying, that you do not burn them; and never make any cautery on the bone of the thumb, and one on the bone of the stomach, and one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And the more you do cauterization, the less you should assist, and it benefits him; and know that the hairs do not feel pain as the healthy ones do, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cauterization be large and small according to the members and the joints, as you will find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the limb with flour and honey and other cures until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When inflammation comes to any member and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then cauterize the member according to its size and smallness; and let the cauterization be a little within the skin of the cure; then treat the wounds until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never cauterize the hand, arm, or back with fire, at the end of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus it becomes stiff and swollen; and in any case, do not interfere unless you are knowledgeable about the limbs and their movements.
de albaras	I'm sorry, I don't understand the phrase
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awake, and medical treatment is of no use, then cauterize it with a small fire, according to the quantity of the curdled milk, until the swelling is hardened and its color changed; then treat it with flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and sand from colon and sand from almond, each in equal parts; and mix them all together, and apply it to the affected area, and bandage it with a cloth, and keep it to the body until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of chancre by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When chancre appears at the beginning, and you see it stop spreading, then cauterize it with a cautery that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And all the wise say that one should also make a cautery in the middle of the chancre; and I do not think it is good because I believe it will become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen this happen; and moreover, the better thing is to cauterize around it, with a cautery that is called «circle», as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the flea bite that cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When anyone has a disease called "adubelati", and it takes a long time to die, either due to the excess it causes or because of the age of the patient when they are elderly (that is, too old) and have little blood, or due to the intensity; then you see it approaching death: therefore cauterize around with many small cauteries by pricking; after leaving it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will approach death.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it perforated with the entire cauteries, then heat the cauteries in this way:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries have pierced through, and be such cauteries that the hairs feel afterwards in such a way that the course of the fever is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure until they are completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The cure of fever by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing other than a kind of member, because it twists the members as if the dry reeds did.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the leg that can suffer cauteries together with fire, then heat the cauteries with a small and large clavile, according to what is needed for the leg or the disease; after cauterizing all parts until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that all that is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let it rest for three days, and apply a cautery above the wounds with oil until the scars of the fire are removed, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns, wounds arise.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if you see after three days that healthy wounds do not arise, it is good; and if not, if the cautery is applied again above the remaining corrupt parts.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this method has never been treated with medicine in place of the fire cauterization; but the fire cauterization is of greater help, and I have already mentioned the treatment of the medicine in the division: take it when you have the opportunity.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the pea-like things that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times, these pea-like things come to the feet through defecation, and a disease arises that is called "clos" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that becomes in the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries of this disease are thus in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to say, fire cauterization, and cauterization with hot iron.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is that you heat the cauterizer like a quill, and it should be made of good iron at the measure that it can penetrate the nail from all parts, and that it has thin margins; afterwards, put it all hot on the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches the base of the nail; and leave it in this way for three days until it begins to rot; then make an ointment of wild savage herbs boiled with oil, and leave the ointment all night, and the nail will fall off and will be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then, treat the joint with heat by applying a hot poultice until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	And if they are converted by the previous heat, and often in hands and feet, it is necessary to apply fire cauterization of hot charcoal; and this is done as follows: take an iron nail or iron, or a pen of wood, and place it on the nail and the wart, that is to say, the warts; then put a little hot water, and hold your hand well, and press your hand in turning so that the edge of the nail comes to the root of the nail, and find the hot charcoal deeply through the root; and let the pain of the hot charcoal for an hour; then leave it thus, and it will all come out at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Then make another one, until you have recovered all those that are in the body, then treat the wounds that generate pus which causes harm.
li cure dou trembler	The cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	When anyone trembles from cold or shivering, or from a quarterly fever or other, it is necessary that you make four cautery burns or four on the backbone; one between each spine; and one on the chest, and one on the stomach at the cautery oil gland; if it allows the trembling, and hastens the recovery from the illness of cold.
des pustules puans	of pus-filled wounds
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No times appear from previous experiences of a bloated body, or pustules that come from large corrupted matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to do a fire cauterization on each pustule head when they appear: a subtle fire cautery of mullein, with which the point can be grasped in the fire, or from the root of aristolochia long, or with the lenticular cauterization.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And no times do they cauterize at the beginning when they appear, in this way, and it cannot grow more, but is broken down from the excess from which they come, and are healed; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	often occurs great bleeding from the artery that is cut at the wound which comes to the periphery, or to the incision of the abscess, or in burning of the limb, and similar things; and it is a very painful thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And whenever this happens to anyone, you must quickly place your second finger on the wound of the vein, and press it very tightly until the blood is no longer coming out, and there is no more dripping; then put the cauteries of olive oil many times small and large as they are all red; then take I, or great or small according to the wound and the limb in which the artery is routed, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cautery there until the bleeding is stopped.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if you lift the other end of the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, quickly take the other hot cautery that is at the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood is stopped; and be careful not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and that no other harm comes over the wound; and make sure that when the artery is cut off, it cannot be stopped immediately if the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods that we have mentioned: by cautery, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by a very gentle thread, or by medicines placed on which have power to stop blood.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will manage the tightening of ropes or other things burning above, or similar things, does not benefit unless it is done carefully.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have any remedy present, they should place their finger index above the wound of the vein as we have said, and tightly bind it until it is tightened above the wound and above the vein; and they should not move it, but keep it cold with cold water often until it is frozen and swollen and tightened; and make inquiries about what they need for cauterizing and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This is the second book of remedies for tails
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have already told you in the first book of all diseases where it is necessary to cauterize with fire, or with burning medicine, and the symptoms and causes and tools and forms of cauteries; and I will put this chapter of the loins from the head down to the feet, and I will go into this chapter by that same way in order to find more easily what we want.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore when I begin this chapter, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for this reason it requires greater caution.
